    <div id="mainContent">
     <!-- InstanceBeginEditable name="MainContent" --> 
     <p align="center"><img src="images/facilities.jpg" alt="CHASS Facilities" width="650" height="300" class="photoborder" /></p> 
     <p>CHASS Facilities Management provides the following services:</p> 
     <ul class="big_arrow"> 
      <li><strong>Event Support: <br /> </strong>CFM provides event management support and coordinate meeting, conference, performance, lecture and screening events. Our office can provide on site event assistance (as needed at a cost). We can provide ushers, room attendants, ticket takers, audio visual technicians. </li> 
      <li><strong>Academic Support:</strong> <br /> CFM will provide audio visual support and set-up assistance to designated CHASS classrooms. We assist with audio visual installation design. CFM can also provide troubleshooting of existing audio visual systems.</li> 
      <li><strong>Access Control:<br /> </strong>CHASS Facilities Management can assist with key management and access card implementation. </li> 
      <li><strong>Safety:<br /> </strong>CFM oversees the safety for CHASS. &nbsp;CFM coordinates with UCR EH&amp;S, UCPD and Physical Plant to define a cohesive safety structure.</li> 
      <li><strong>Facility Maintenance and Project Management: </strong> <br /> CFM can provide support for facilities alterations. CHASS Facilities Management will assist with coordination of scheduling of work, budget controls, and Physical Plant/contractor interaction. CFM can also assist with coordination of scheduled maintenance.</li> 
      <li><strong>Space Management:<br /> </strong>CHASS Facilities Management will assist with department relocations. CFM provides assistance with space reporting (UCR FMS) and acquisition of space. </li> 
     </ul>

     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">External Relations</h1> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We build public understanding and support for the university's mission.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>External Relations is focused on establishing strong relationships with outside constituencies and building broad understanding of the many ways in which UC contributes to the lives of all Californians. Departments within External Relations are responsible for communications, governmental relations at the state and federal levels, and institutional advocacy.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="Daniel M. Dooley" src="_files/shot_29_ddooley_023.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> <a href="daniel-m.-dooley.html">Daniel M. Dooley</a> </p> 
         <p>Senior Vice President</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/er_org_chart.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row-fluid blustripe dept-unit"> 
      <h2 class="nobtm">DEPARTMENTS</h2> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/alumni-constituent-affairs/index.html">Alumni and Constituent Affairs</a> </h3> 
        <p>Increases the involvement of alumni in supporting UC through support of UC alumni associations and stewardship of the AAUC.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/alumni-constituent-affairs/staff-contacts/index.html">Staff and contacts</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/alumni-constituent-affairs/services-programs/index.html">Alumni and visitor sites</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/alumni-constituent-affairs/support-uc/index.html">Support UC</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/communications/index.html">Communications</a> </h3> 
        <p>Works to build public awareness of UC’s value and its impact on the lives of people in California and beyond.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/communications/what-we-do/index.html">What we do</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/communications/what-we-do/before-you-call.html">Tips for working with us</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/communications/resources/index.html">Tools and guidelines</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/federal-governmental-relations/index.html">Federal Governmental Relations</a> </h3> 
        <p>Works with congress, the administration, federal agencies and national organizations to advocate for the university.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/federal-governmental-relations/staff-liaisons/campus-federal-liaisons/index.html">Campus federal liaisons</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/federal-governmental-relations/policy-legislation/index.html">Issues and policy papers</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/federal-governmental-relations/resources/index.html">Resources</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="row-fluid col5"> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/institutional-advancement/index.html">Institutional Advancement</a> </h3> 
        <p>Facilitates support for UC through private gifts, grants and contracts as well as federal and state appropriations and contracts. </p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/institutional-advancement/reports/index.html">Annual reports on private support</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/institutional-advancement/reports/endowment-reports/index.html">Endowment reports</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/institutional-advancement/policies-and-guidelines/index.html">Inventory of policy and delegation</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/impac/index.html">IMPAC</a> </h3> 
        <p>Develops UC's positions on legislative issues and provides analysis and research in support of policy initiatives.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/impac/legislation/federal-legislation.html">Federal legislation</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/impac/legislation/sponsored-legislation.html">UC-sponsored legislation</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/impac/projects/index.html">Policy initiatives and projects</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
       <div class="span4"> 
        <h3 class="blue"> <a href="/state-governmental-relations/index.html">State Governmental Relations</a> </h3> 
        <p>Serves as the primary university representative to state elected officials and agencies.</p> 
        <dl class="top-dest"> 
         <dt>
          Top Destinations
         </dt> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/state-governmental-relations/legislation/index.html">Legislation</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/state-governmental-relations/budget/index.html">Budget resources</a> 
         </dd> 
         <dd> 
          <a href="/state-governmental-relations/advocacy/index.html">Advocacy</a> 
         </dd> 
        </dl> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="row less3 novrflw"> 
      <div class="span4 grybx"> 
       <h4>Contact us</h4> 
       <p>Phone: (510) 987-0060<br /> <br /> External Relations<br /> University of California<br /> Office of the President<br /> 1111 Franklin Street<br /> Oakland, CA 94607</p> 
       <h4>Media inquiries</h4> 
       <p>Phone: (510) 987-9200</p> 
      </div>

       <p><a href="http://promiseforeducation.org">View details</a></p>

    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };

     <img src="/Images/course-status.jpg" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>Keep Your Courses and Student Status </h3> 
      <p> If your student status lapses, you can lose your courses, student privileges and financial aid. If you are an undergraduate student with lapsed student status, you must apply for <a href="/registrar/registering-for-classes/cancellation-withdrawal-absence-readmission.aspx?tabrequest=readmission">readmission</a> if you want to be reinstated as a UCR student and you must pick up the readmission packet from the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS).</p> 
      <h4>Meet the Fee Payment Deadline </h4> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
       <li>If you don’t pay your tuition and fees by <a href="http://www.sbs.ucr.edu/news.html" target="_blank">the fee payment deadline</a>, you could lose your courses and be charged a $50 late fee.</li> 
       <li>You have the opportunity after losing your courses to re-enroll in classes on a space-available basis and pay your fees.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4>How Does Student Status Lapse? </h4> 
      <p>On Friday night of the third week of instruction your status lapses when:</p> 
      <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
       <li>You fail to pay your tuition and fees, and/or</li> 
       <li>You fail to register. </li> 
      </ul> 
      <p>&nbsp;</p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-7 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <span class="warning">Important</span> 
       <img style="float:right;" src="../../Images/paperpushpin.png" alt="" /> 
       <ul> 
        <li>If you want your financial aid and/or student loans to pay for tuition and fees, <strong>you must be registered for the right amount of units</strong> by the fee payment deadline. Contact <a href="http://financialaid.ucr.edu/Pages/default.aspx">Financial Aid f</a>or details.</li> 
       </ul> 
      </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
